***никто.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никто́</a> (132)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nikъto</i>. <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ni</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никто́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">niktó</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(indefinite pronoun)</i> nobody, no one; <i>(with negative)</i> anybody, anyone
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никого́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>nikovó</b> ne znáju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don’t know anybody.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никто́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Niktó</b> ne znájet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Nobody knows.</span></div>
<dl><dd>but: <div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>Ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ni on, <b>ni kto</b> drugój ne znájet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Neither he <b>nor anyone</b> else knows.</span></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Prepositions are always interposed, dividing the word in two:
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>ni u kovó</b> né byl.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I haven’t visited anybody.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>ке́м</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́т</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>ni s kem</b> ne govorít.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He’s not speaking to anybody.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кто́-либо</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">któ-libo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кто́-нибудь</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">któ-nibudʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кто́-то</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">któ-to</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некто.html>не́кто</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nékto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некого.html>не́кого</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nékovo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто́</a></b>
</p><p>Местоимение, <a href = vnd.unilang:отрицательный.html>отрица́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельное</a>.

***никуда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:никуда.html>никуда́</a> (1656)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:никуда.html>никуда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nikudá</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>nowhere, nowhither
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:никуда.html>никуда́</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>иду́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja nikudá ne idú.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’m not going anywhere.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нигде.html>нигде́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja nigdé né byl.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I haven’t been anywhere.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:никудышный.html>никуды́шный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nikudýšnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)никуды́шнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)никуды́шней</b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bad, useless, in no respect good</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нирвана.html>нирва́на</a> (22263)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">निर्वाण</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nir-vāṇa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">blown or put out, extinguished</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нирвана.html>нирва́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nirvána</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нирвана.html>нирва́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нирвана.html>нирва́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нирвана.html>нирва́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nirvana</li></ol>

***нисколько.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нисколько.html>ниско́лько</a> (3862)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нисколько.html>ниско́лько</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">niskólʹko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>not in the least, not at all, none at all (of quantity)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нисколько.html>ниско́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:трудно.html>тру́дно</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto <b>niskólʹko</b> ne trúdno.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It's not difficult <b>at all</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоить.html>сто́ило</a>? — <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нисколько.html>ниско́лько</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— Skólʹko éto tebé stóilo? — <b>Niskólʹko</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">“How much did it cost you?” “<b>Nothing</b>.”</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>; неизменяемое.

<p><b>нис<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:па.html>па</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́ть</a></b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нить.html>нить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нитка.html>ни́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nítka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нитка.html>ни́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нитка.html>ни́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нитка.html>ни́ток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thread
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>ши́тый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лыми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нитка.html>ни́тками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">šítyj bélymi nítkami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">transparent, obvious to anyone</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">sewn with white threads</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>string <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of beads</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ниточка.html>ни́точка</a> (7970)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нитка.html>ни́тка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nítka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ниточка.html>ни́точка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nítočka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ниточка.html>ни́точки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ниточка.html>ни́точки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ниточка.html>ни́точек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нить.html>нить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>, <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нитка.html>ни́тка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nítka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (short or thin) thread
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ниточка.html>ни́точке</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xodítʹ po <b>nítočke</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to toe the line; to do as one is told</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ничегошеньки.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничегошеньки.html>ничего́шеньки</a> (22111)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничегошеньки.html>ничего́шеньки</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ničegóšenʹki</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nothing at all, not a thing</li></ol>

***ничком.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничком.html>ничко́м</a> (11812)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ниц.html>ниц</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nic</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:никнуть.html>ни́кнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">níknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">ни́шком</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nýškom</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничком.html>ни́чком</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">níčkom</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничком.html>ничко́м</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ničkóm</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>prone, face down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежа́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ничком.html>ничко́м</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ležátʹ <b>ničkóm</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lie prone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>нич<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>ко́м</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>, определительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:образ.html>образа</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:способ.html>спо́соба</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствия</a>; неизменяемое.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-нич-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ком</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вниз.html>вниз</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земле́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>полу</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen"><a href = vnd.unilang:буратино.html>Буратино</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упасть.html>упа́л</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничком.html>ничко́м</a></span>, — <a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>нос</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глубокий.html>глубоко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воткнуться.html>воткну́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>зе́млю</a>. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%A2%D0%BE%D0%BB%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B9,_%D0%90%D0%BB%D0%B5%D0%BA%D1%81%D0%B5%D0%B9_%D0%9D%D0%B8%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:Толстой, Алексей Николаевич">A. ***ничто.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничто́</a> (84)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ni</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štó</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">what</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничто́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ništó</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(indefinite pronoun)</i> nothing
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничто́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ло</a> (o чём-либо).</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ništó</b> ne govorílo (o čóm-libo).</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Nothing</b> foretold (of something).</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The nominative and accusative are usually replaced by the genitive <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ničevó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in common speech.</li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что́</a></b>
</p><p>Местоименное <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:отрицательный.html>отрица́тельное</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сочетание.html>сочета́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>предло́гами</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:писаться.html>пи́шется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздельно.html>разде́льно</a>: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>чем</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чём</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> т.п.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>ни-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-что-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***ничтожество.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничтожество.html>ничто́жество</a> (11552)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничтожество.html>ничто́жество</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ničtóžestvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничтожество.html>ничто́жества</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничтожество.html>ничто́жества</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничтожество.html>ничто́жеств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nonentity <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an unimportant or insignificant person</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>smallness, pettiness, nothingness</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:жест.html>жест</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a></b>

***ничтожный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничтожный.html>ничто́жный</a> (5397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничтожный.html>ничто́жный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ničtóžnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>trifling, insignificant, contemptible</li>
<li>worthless, paltry, despicable, mean
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ничтожный.html>ничто́жный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:трус.html>трус</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ničtóžnyj</b> trus</i> ― <span class="e-translation">paltry coward</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> null and void</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничтожество.html>ничто́жество</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ničtóžestvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>что́ж<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>ничто́жнее.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>ни-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-что-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ж-н</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***ничья.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничья.html>ничья́</a> (12460)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничья.html>ничья́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игра́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ničʹjá igrá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nobody's game</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нищета.html>нищета́</a> (7231)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нищета.html>нищета́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">niščetá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нищета.html>нищеты́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>poverty, destitution, penury, misery
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1886</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Chekhov</a>,  “The Chorus Girl”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:средство.html>сре́дство</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спасти.html>спасти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нищета.html>нищеты́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:позор.html>позо́ра</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">A méždu tem jestʹ srédstvo spastí jevó i nas ot <b>niščetý</b> i pozóra.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And yet there is a chance of saving him and us from <b>destitution</b> and disgrace.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>beggars, beggary</li></ol>

***нищий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нищий.html>ни́щий</a> (15660)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*niščь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нищий.html>ни́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">níščij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:нищий.html>нище́е</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:нищий.html>нище́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>poor, beggarly, destitute</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нищий.html>ни́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">níščij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нищий.html>ни́щего</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нищий.html>ни́щие</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нищий.html>ни́щих</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>beggar, pauper</li></ol>

***но.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> (17)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*nu</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">now</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">num</i> ("now") and <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">nunc</i> (lt; *num + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ce</i>, "now").
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_3">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">no</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>but, yet</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">no</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>but
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>Есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>ма́ленькое</a> «<b><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но́</a></b>»</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jestʹ málenʹkoje “<b>nó</b>”</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There is a slight objection.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:никакой.html>никаки́х</a> «<b><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но́</a></b>»!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nikakíx “<b>nó</b>”!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">But me no buts!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
